Here are some common types of fantasy settings:\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"1. **Medieval Fantasy:**\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"- Often inspired by medieval Europe, this setting features castles, knights, dragons, and magical elements. It's a classic backdrop for epic quests and tales of chivalry.\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"2. **Urban Fantasy:**\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"- Set in contemporary or modern cities with a magical or supernatural twist. The magical elements coexist with everyday life, and protagonists navigate both the mundane and magical aspects of the world.\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"3. **High Fantasy:**\\\", \\\"modifiers\\\": {}}], \\\"indent\\\": 0, \\\"quoted\\\": false, \\\"type\\\": \\\"plain\\\", \\\"is_rtl\\\": false}, {\\\"spans\\\": [{\\\"text\\\": \\\"- Characterized by grand and immersive world-building, high fantasy often involves complex histories, multiple races, and intricate magical systems.
